NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

eloborate sexual reassignment surgery by Dr. Jayaraman. V MS. Mch. MNAMS. Dip.N.B, Phd.,FICS. Former Professor head,
KMCH, Chennai-600 010.
By this, I, may be treated as a male and shall henceforth be known as SIVANANDHU.T
Chennai,
18th July 2017.

SUBHA. L alias SHUBHA THANKAPPAN

1991, residing at No. 1/46, M.G.R. Street, Mannivakkam, Chennai-600 048, shall henceforth be
known as D. GOPALAKRISHNAN.
